<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вълна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭlna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьlna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">вльна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlĭna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">вълна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vǎlna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">vlna</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">vlna</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">wełna</i>. <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волны́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>во́лны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>во́лн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wave</li>
<li>wavelength</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьlna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂wĺ̥h₁neh₂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>во́лна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volná</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vólna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волны́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>во́лны</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wool of sheep or goats</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вол.html>вол</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1d  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1f: мн. ч. — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́м</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́ми</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́х</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-волн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.

***волнение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́ние</a> (2248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(at sea)</i> choppiness, roughness</li>
<li>excitement, tizzy
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “The Chorus Girl”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барыня.html>ба́рыня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льном</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́нии</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройтись.html>прошла́сь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bárynja vstála i v sílʹnom <b>volnénii</b> prošlásʹ po kómnate.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The lady got up and walked about the room in great <b>excitement</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>unrest, riot, civil commotion</li></ol>

***волновать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ть</a> (3691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volnovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взволновать.html>взволнова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to agitate, to trouble, to excite, to stir, to disturb, to worry, to alarm, to upset</li>
<li>to ruffle, to stir</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волноваться.html>волнова́ться</a> (1726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">volnovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волноваться.html>волнова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volnovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взволноваться.html>взволнова́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заволноваться.html>заволнова́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поволнова́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to worry, to be upset, to be agitated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:волноваться.html>волну́юсь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja tak <b>volnújusʹ</b> za tebjá!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm so <b>worried</b> for you!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ripple, to be rough (<i>waves</i>), to billow, to surge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:волноваться.html>волну́ется</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móre <b>volnújetsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The sea is <b>surging</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">volnovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вол.html>вол</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

Зализняка — 2a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:взволноваться.html>взволнова́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:заволноваться.html>заволнова́ться</a>, поволноваться.

***волос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>волос</a> (570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*volsъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">влас</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic. From <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hair; wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p><p>Cognates with ￼￼￼￼￼￼￼Old Persian￼￼ (vars), Persian گرس‎ (gurs, “curled hair”), Kurdish <i>pirç</i> (“hair”) and Lithuanian <i>￼￼valaĩ￼￼,</i> Sanskrit￼￼￼￼￼￼￼￼ वल्श (válśa, “twig, sprout). Akin to Old Armenian վարս (vars), an Iranian borrowing.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лос</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vólos</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лоса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>воло́с</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a hair</li></ol>

Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуются</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лость</a> (30262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">volostĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*volstь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlastʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">power, authority</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vólostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>волосте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> volost, district, county</li></ol>

***волочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волочить.html>волочи́ть</a> (7658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*volčiti</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влачить.html>влачи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlačítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волочить.html>волочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voločítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уволочь.html>уволо́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проволочи́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уволочи́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drag, to trail</li>
<li>to draw</li></ol>

***волочь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волочь.html>воло́чь</a> (11366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*velťi</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волочь.html>воло́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volóčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поволочь.html>поволо́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приволочь.html>приволо́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уволочь.html>уволо́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drag, to haul, to draw</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:волшба.html>волшба́</a> (31904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вълшьба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭlšĭba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъlšьba</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъlšiti</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">влъснѫти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlŭsnǫti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волшба.html>волшба́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volšbá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волшба.html>волшбы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> magic, sorcery</li></ol>
